        <script type="text/javascript">//<![CDATA[
  function external_links_in_new_windows_loop() {
    if (!document.links) {
      document.links = document.getElementsByTagName('a');
    }
    var change_link = false;
    var force = '';
    var ignore = '';

    for (var t=0; t<document.links.length; t++) {
      var all_links = document.links[t];
      change_link = false;
      
      if(document.links[t].hasAttribute('onClick') == false) {
        // forced if the address starts with http (or also https), but does not link to the current domain
        if(all_links.href.search(/^http/) != -1 && all_links.href.search('britonthemove.com') == -1 && all_links.href.search(/^#/) == -1) {
          // console.log('Changed ' + all_links.href);
          change_link = true;
        }
          
        if(force != '' && all_links.href.search(force) != -1) {
          // forced
          // console.log('force ' + all_links.href);
          change_link = true;
        }
        
        if(ignore != '' && all_links.href.search(ignore) != -1) {
          // console.log('ignore ' + all_links.href);
          // ignored
          change_link = false;
        }

        if(change_link == true) {
          // console.log('Changed ' + all_links.href);
          document.links[t].setAttribute('onClick', 'javascript:window.open(\'' + all_links.href.replace(/'/g, '') + '\', \'_blank\', \'noopener\'); return false;');
          document.links[t].removeAttribute('target');
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  // Load
  function external_links_in_new_windows_load(func)
  {  
    var oldonload = window.onload;
    if (typeof window.onload != 'function'){
      window.onload = func;
    } else {
      window.onload = function(){
        oldonload();
        func();
      }
    }
  }

  external_links_in_new_windows_load(external_links_in_new_windows_loop);
  //]]></script>

				<article id="post-2" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-2 page type-page status-publish has-post-thumbnail hentry mv-content-wrapper">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id2_47ee06-75 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-left-golden kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_c56c17-b9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color">Welcome to Brit On The Move™, travel tips dedicated to helping you escape the office and travel more for less.</h1>



<h6 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color">Nikki Webster is a solo travel writer who covers how to travel the world without breaking the bank using clever travel hacks that save thousands. <strong>&nbsp;</strong></h6>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color"><strong>A fan of off-the-beaten-track experiences, glamping, and water. She splits her time between <a href="https://britonthemove.com/florida/">Florida</a>, England, and Scotland when not on the road.</strong></h4>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color"><strong>Hailing from the UK, she passionately writes about experiences in England and Scotland. She is particularly fond of Florida, writing about its sprigs, beaches, national parks, and many other experiences beyond the theme parks. &nbsp;</strong></h4>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color"><strong>Nikki flies around 60,000 miles annually and has visited 80 <a href="https://britonthemove.com/how-many-countries-in-the-world/">countries</a>, 50 states, and six continents.</strong></h4>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns2_c083ce-c2"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn2_b46bad-13 kt-btn-size-large kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-true  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://britonthemove.com/resources/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Start Here</span><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_arrowRight kt-btn-icon-side-right"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/><polyline points="12 5 19 12 12 19"/></svg></span></a></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_ae64d6-e1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><picture><source srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Brit-On-The-Move-Peru.webp 700w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Brit-On-The-Move-Peru-205x300.webp 205w" sizes="(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" type="image/webp"><img src="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Brit-On-The-Move-Peru.jpg" height="1022" width="700" srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Brit-On-The-Move-Peru.jpg 700w, https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Brit-On-The-Move-Peru-205x300.jpg 205w" sizes="(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px" class="wp-image-48704 sp-no-webp" alt="Travel Tips By Brit On The Move " fetchpriority="high" decoding="async"  > </picture></figure>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id2_ac5c16-12 alignfull kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_ffd744-c6"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading2_ad9505-d3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_ad9505-d3"> <strong><strong> Travel Tips, <strong><strong>Travel Hacks,</strong></strong> &amp; Travel Deals </strong></strong>&#8211; <strong><strong> Brit On The Move™</strong></strong></h1>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-2_1386e4-3d"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div>



<p>I am Nikki. A professional travel writer who loves adventure lives for off-the-beaten-track experiences and calls <a href="https://britonthemove.com/category/florida/">Florida</a> and England home while exploring the world.</p>



<p class="has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color">By day, you’ll find me on some crazy adventures like swimming with sharks in the Galapagos Islands, navigating Florida’s coastline on my boat, kayaking the Florida springs, or exploring the <a class="wpil_keyword_link" title="English" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" href="https://britonthemove.com/britlish/">English</a> countryside, sampling a variety of glamping sites. By night, I’m often around a fire or seeking night-themed adventures like night <a class="wpil_keyword_link" title="fishing" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" href="https://britonthemove.com/florida-fishing-license/">fishing</a>, skinny dipping, or soaking in wood-burning hot tubs.</p>



<p class="has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color">If you’re looking for an online publication and community that focuses on how to travel more for less using a variety of travel hacks and exploring lesser-known attractions, you’ve come to the right place. &nbsp;This award-winning travel publication and community is all about <a class="wpil_keyword_link" title="adrenaline" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked" href="https://britonthemove.com/sand-dunes-in-michigan/">adrenaline</a> adventures, unusual accommodations, and weird and wonderful experiences.</p>


<div class="grow-inline-subscribe-widget-e563b92c-aa0b-4df5-9ced-f3addeccc1b8"></div>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id2_778959-19 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_2bb0b5-ae"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center" id="h-brit-on-the-move-will-help-you"><strong>Brit on the Move™ will help you:</strong></h2>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Master the travel tips that professional travelers use to travel the world</li>



<li>Learn how to travel using&nbsp;<a href="https://britonthemove.com/20-best-ways-to-earn-lots-of-credit-card-rewards-points/">points</a>&nbsp;from credit cards and loyalty programs</li>



<li>Discover how to find the best travel deals that accomplish your travel goals</li>



<li>Gain expert knowledge and travel tips about destinations you are considering</li>



<li>Get genuine <a class="wpil_keyword_link" href="https://britonthemove.com/the-best-travel-tips/" title="travel tips" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked">travel tips</a>, honest reviews, and advice – for FREE</li>
</ul>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_8c94fa-2f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><strong>Brit on the Move™&nbsp;<em>will not</em>:</strong></h2>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Share articles or content that is biased, skewed, or misleading</li>



<li>Try to sell you the dream of traveling the world for free, or try to make you believe that is an easy task</li>



<li>Attempt to convince you to quit your job and become a digital nomad</li>



<li>Email you spam and useless information that clogs your email.</li>



<li>Encourage you to start a website or blog</li>
</ul>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id2_ec1b9c-17 alignfull kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_ecca0f-c0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading2_df2409-4c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_df2409-4c"><strong><strong><strong>Brit On The Move’s™ Philosophy</strong></strong></strong></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id2_92c6bf-9d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-center-half kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_f7c224-30"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><picture><source srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.avif 200w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-150x150.avif 150w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-66x66.avif 66w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" type="image/avif"><source srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.webp 200w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-150x150.webp 150w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-66x66.webp 66w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" type="image/webp"><img src="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.jpg" height="200" width="200" srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.jpg 200w, https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-150x150.jpg 150w, https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-66x66.jpg 66w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" class="wp-image-34576 sp-no-webp" alt="Brit On The Move Favicon" loading="lazy" decoding="async"  > </picture></figure>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_8b018a-78"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-accordion alignnone"><div class="kt-accordion-wrap kt-accordion-id2_7b186d-82 kt-accordion-has-37-panes kt-active-pane-0 kt-accordion-block kt-pane-header-alignment-left kt-accodion-icon-style-arrow kt-accodion-icon-side-right" style="max-width:none"><div class="kt-accordion-inner-wrap" data-allow-multiple-open="false" data-start-open="0">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-1 kt-pane2_a9ca79-97"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Brit On The Move™ Philosophy</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>You only get one life, and tomorrow is not guaranteed. Many people wait for retirement to travel the world. What if you are not lucky enough to make it to retirement? The ability to travel boils down to priorities. Do you need a new car? How big of a home do you need? Travel is the greatest education money can buy and the foundation of freedom and adventure.</p>



<p>Live in the moment……….Live now!</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane2_4b164a-b1"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Brit On The Move™ Mission</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>To inspire individuals to live every day to its fullest and travel the world as much as possible.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane2_1bc331-0e"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>Brit On The Move™ Promise</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>To provide accurate travel tips, honest advice, and reviews that make a difference or solve real problems travelers face.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_8d3cef-c0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><picture><source srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.avif 200w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-150x150.avif 150w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-66x66.avif 66w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" type="image/avif"><source srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.webp 200w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-150x150.webp 150w,https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-66x66.webp 66w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" type="image/webp"><img src="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.jpg" height="200" width="200" srcset="https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon.jpg 200w, https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-150x150.jpg 150w, https://britonthemove.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Brit-On-The-Move-Favicon-66x66.jpg 66w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" class="wp-image-34576 sp-no-webp" alt="Brit On The Move Favicon" loading="lazy" decoding="async"  > </picture></figure>
